   <script type="text/javascript">
    //<![CDATA[
 
 /**
  * jQuery Mobile Menu 
  * Turn unordered list menu into dropdown select menu
  * version 1.0(31-OCT-2011)
  * 
  * Built on top of the jQuery library
  *   http://jquery.com
  * 
  * Documentation
  * 	 http://github.com/mambows/mobilemenu
  */
 (function($){
 $.fn.mobileMenu = function(options) {
 	
 	var defaults = {
 			defaultText: 'Navigate to...',
 			className: 'select-menu',
 			containerClass: 'select-menu-container',
 			subMenuClass: 'sub-menu',
 			subMenuDash: '&ndash;'
 		},
 		settings = $.extend( defaults, options ),
 		el = $(this);
 	
 	this.each(function(){
 		// ad class to submenu list
 		el.find('ul').addClass(settings.subMenuClass);
 
         // Create base menu
 		$('<div />',{
 			'class' : settings.containerClass
 		}).insertAfter( el );
         
 		// Create base menu
 		$('<select />',{
 			'class' : settings.className
 		}).appendTo( '.' + settings.containerClass );
 
 		// Create default option
 		$('<option />', {
 			"value"		: '#',
 			"text"		: settings.defaultText
 		}).appendTo( '.' + settings.className );
 
 		// Create select option from menu
 		el.find('a').each(function(){
 			var $this 	= $(this),
 					optText	= '&nbsp;' + $this.text(),
 					optSub	= $this.parents( '.' + settings.subMenuClass ),
 					len			= optSub.length,
 					dash;
 			
 			// if menu has sub menu
 			if( $this.parents('ul').hasClass( settings.subMenuClass ) ) {
 				dash = Array( len+1 ).join( settings.subMenuDash );
 				optText = dash + optText;
 			}
 
 			// Now build menu and append it
 			$('<option />', {
 				"value"	: this.href,
 				"html"	: optText,
 				"selected" : (this.href == window.location.href)
 			}).appendTo( '.' + settings.className );
 
 		}); // End el.find('a').each
 
 		// Change event on select element
 		$('.' + settings.className).change(function(){
 			var locations = $(this).val();
 			if( locations !== '#' ) {
 				window.location.href = $(this).val();
 			};
 		});
 
 	}); // End this.each
 
 	return this;
 
 };
 })(jQuery);

   <script type="text/javascript">
    //<![CDATA[
 
 (function($){
 	/* hoverIntent by Brian Cherne */
 	$.fn.hoverIntent = function(f,g) {
 		// default configuration options
 		var cfg = {
 			sensitivity: 7,
 			interval: 100,
 			timeout: 0
 		};
 		// override configuration options with user supplied object
 		cfg = $.extend(cfg, g ? { over: f, out: g } : f );
 
 		// instantiate variables
 		// cX, cY = current X and Y position of mouse, updated by mousemove event
 		// pX, pY = previous X and Y position of mouse, set by mouseover and polling interval
 		var cX, cY, pX, pY;
 
 		// A private function for getting mouse position
 		var track = function(ev) {
 			cX = ev.pageX;
 			cY = ev.pageY;
 		};
 
 		// A private function for comparing current and previous mouse position
 		var compare = function(ev,ob) {
 			ob.hoverIntent_t = clearTimeout(ob.hoverIntent_t);
 			// compare mouse positions to see if they've crossed the threshold
 			if ( ( Math.abs(pX-cX) + Math.abs(pY-cY) ) < cfg.sensitivity ) {
 				$(ob).unbind("mousemove",track);
 				// set hoverIntent state to true (so mouseOut can be called)
 				ob.hoverIntent_s = 1;
 				return cfg.over.apply(ob,[ev]);
 			} else {
 				// set previous coordinates for next time
 				pX = cX; pY = cY;
 				// use self-calling timeout, guarantees intervals are spaced out properly (avoids JavaScript timer bugs)
 				ob.hoverIntent_t = setTimeout( function(){compare(ev, ob);} , cfg.interval );
 			}
 		};
 
 		// A private function for delaying the mouseOut function
 		var delay = function(ev,ob) {
 			ob.hoverIntent_t = clearTimeout(ob.hoverIntent_t);
 			ob.hoverIntent_s = 0;
 			return cfg.out.apply(ob,[ev]);
 		};
 
 		// A private function for handling mouse 'hovering'
 		var handleHover = function(e) {
 			// next three lines copied from jQuery.hover, ignore children onMouseOver/onMouseOut
 			var p = (e.type == "mouseover" ? e.fromElement : e.toElement) || e.relatedTarget;
 			while ( p && p != this ) { try { p = p.parentNode; } catch(e) { p = this; } }
 			if ( p == this ) { return false; }
 
 			// copy objects to be passed into t (required for event object to be passed in IE)
 			var ev = jQuery.extend({},e);
 			var ob = this;
 
 			// cancel hoverIntent timer if it exists
 			if (ob.hoverIntent_t) { ob.hoverIntent_t = clearTimeout(ob.hoverIntent_t); }
 
 			// else e.type == "onmouseover"
 			if (e.type == "mouseover") {
 				// set "previous" X and Y position based on initial entry point
 				pX = ev.pageX; pY = ev.pageY;
 				// update "current" X and Y position based on mousemove
 				$(ob).bind("mousemove",track);
 				// start polling interval (self-calling timeout) to compare mouse coordinates over time
 				if (ob.hoverIntent_s != 1) { ob.hoverIntent_t = setTimeout( function(){compare(ev,ob);} , cfg.interval );}
 
 			// else e.type == "onmouseout"
 			} else {
 				// unbind expensive mousemove event
 				$(ob).unbind("mousemove",track);
 				// if hoverIntent state is true, then call the mouseOut function after the specified delay
 				if (ob.hoverIntent_s == 1) { ob.hoverIntent_t = setTimeout( function(){delay(ev,ob);} , cfg.timeout );}
 			}
 		};
 
 		// bind the function to the two event listeners
 		return this.mouseover(handleHover).mouseout(handleHover);
 	};
 	
 })(jQuery);
 
 //]]>
   </script>

 /*

 ;(function($){
 	$.fn.superfish = function(op){
 
 		var sf = $.fn.superfish,
 			c = sf.c,
 			$arrow = $(['<span class="',c.arrowClass,'"> &#187;</span>'].join('')),
 			over = function(){
 				var $$ = $(this), menu = getMenu($$);

 			},
 			out = function(){
 				var $$ = $(this), menu = getMenu($$), o = sf.op;
 				clearTimeout(menu.sfTimer);
 				menu.sfTimer=setTimeout(function(){
 					o.retainPath=($.inArray($$[0],o.$path)>-1);
 					$$.hideSuperfishUl();

 				},o.delay);	
 			},
 			getMenu = function($menu){

 			},

 			$(this).addClass(menuClasses.join(' '));
 		});
 	};
 
 	var sf = $.fn.superfish;
 	sf.o = [];
 	sf.op = {};

 			this.toggleClass(sf.c.shadowClass+'-off');
 		};
 	sf.c = {
 		bcClass     : 'sf-breadcrumb',
 		menuClass   : 'sf-js-enabled',
 		anchorClass : 'sf-with-ul',
 		arrowClass  : 'sf-sub-indicator',
 		shadowClass : 'sf-shadow'
 	};
 	sf.defaults = {
 		hoverClass	: 'sfHover',
 		pathClass	: 'overideThisToUse',
 		pathLevels	: 1,
 		delay		: 200,
 		animation	: {opacity:'show'},
 		speed		: 'normal',
 		autoArrows	: true,
 		dropShadows : true,
 		disableHI	: false,		// true disables hoverIntent detection
 		onInit		: function(){}, // callback functions
 		onBeforeShow: function(){},
 		onShow		: function(){},
 		onHide		: function(){}
 	};
 	$.fn.extend({
 		hideSuperfishUl : function(){
 			var o = sf.op,
 				not = (o.retainPath===true) ? o.$path : '';
 			o.retainPath = false;
 			var $ul = $(['li.',o.hoverClass].join(''),this).add(this).not(not).removeClass(o.hoverClass)
 					.find('>ul').hide().css('visibility','hidden');
 			o.onHide.call($ul);
 			return this;
 		},
 		showSuperfishUl : function(){
 			var o = sf.op,
 				sh = sf.c.shadowClass+'-off',
 				$ul = this.addClass(o.hoverClass)
 					.find('>ul:hidden').css('visibility','visible');
 			sf.IE7fix.call($ul);
 			o.onBeforeShow.call($ul);
 			$ul.animate(o.animation,o.speed,function(){ sf.IE7fix.call($ul); o.onShow.call($ul); });
 			return this;
 		}
 	});
 
 })(jQuery);

   <script type="text/javascript">

 (function($){var ver="2.88";if($.support==undefined){$.support={opacity:!($.browser.msie)};}function debug(s){if($.fn.cycle.debug){log(s);}}function exposeAddSlide(opts,els){opts.addSlide=function(newSlide,prepend){var    <script type="text/javascript">
    //<![CDATA[
 
 function removeHtmlTag(strx,chop){ 
 	if(strx.indexOf("<")!=-1)
 	{
 		var s = strx.split("<"); 
 		for(var i=0;i<s.length;i++){ 
 			if(s[i].indexOf(">")!=-1){ 
 				s[i] = s[i].substring(s[i].indexOf(">")+1,s[i].length); 
 			} 
 		} 
 		strx =  s.join(""); 
 	}
 	chop = (chop < strx.length-1) ? chop : strx.length-2; 
 	while(strx.charAt(chop-1)!=' ' && strx.indexOf(' ',chop)!=-1) chop++; 
 	strx = strx.substring(0,chop-1); 
 	return strx+'...'; 
 }
 
 function createSummaryAndThumb(pID){
 	var div = document.getElementById(pID);
 	var imgtag = "";
 	var img = div.getElementsByTagName("img");
 	var summ = summary_noimg;
 	if(img.length>=1) {	
 		imgtag = '<img src="'+img[0].src+'" width="'+img_thumb_width+'px" height="'+img_thumb_height+'px" style="float:left;margin:0px 10px 5px 0px;padding:6px;border:1px solid #eee;background:#ffffff;"/>';
 		summ = summary_img;
 	}
 	
 	var summary = imgtag + '<div>' + removeHtmlTag(div.innerHTML,summ) + '</div>';
 	div.innerHTML = summary;
 }
 
 //]]>
   </script>

           <div class="date-outer">
            <h2 class="date-header">
             <span>
              Friday, July 20, 2018
             </span>
            </h2>
            <div class="date-posts">
             <div class="post-outer">
              <div class="wrapfullpost">
               <div class="post hentry">
                <a name="2718390232636884110">
                </a>
                <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                 <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/07/why-39-million-for-zack-steffen-is-not.html">
                  Why $3.9 million for Zack Steffen is not enough for the Columbus Crew to say "yes" currently.
                 </a>
                </h3>
                <div class="post-header-line-1">
                </div>
                <div class="postmeta-primary">
                 <span class="meta_date">
                  5:03 AM
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_categories">
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_comments">
                  <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/07/why-39-million-for-zack-steffen-is-not.html#comment-form" onclick="">
                   No comments
                  </a>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="post-body entry-content">
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <div id="summary2718390232636884110">
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                   <a href="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-yadI7fyX8mc/W1HNnHHly-I/AAAAAAAAGSg/1j56yfZt4xkxW6oADvLt4bzXuPTl3VgAACLcBGAs/s1600/bristol.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                    <img border="0" data-original-height="1067" data-original-width="1600" height="426" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-yadI7fyX8mc/W1HNnHHly-I/AAAAAAAAGSg/1j56yfZt4xkxW6oADvLt4bzXuPTl3VgAACLcBGAs/s640/bristol.png" width="640"/>
                   </a>
                  </div>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   The Bristol Post highlighted the rationale here for why the Columbus Crew didn't accept the $3.9 million offer for Zack Steffen yesterday from Bristol City.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-lang="en">
                   <div dir="ltr" lang="und">
                    <a href="https://t.co/uLMW9uZxRe">
                     https://t.co/uLMW9uZxRe
                    </a>
                   </div>
                   — CREWTURE.NET (@crewture)
                   <a href="https://twitter.com/crewture/status/1020134936991367175?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                    July 20, 2018
                   </a>
                  </blockquote>
                  <script async="" charset="utf-8" src="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js">
                  </script>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   They highlight
                   <a href="https://www.massivereport.com/2018/7/19/17590692/selling-zack-steffen-now-does-not-make-sense-for-columbus-crew-sc">
                    The Massive Report's
                   </a>
                   rationalization: "With the way MLS transfer rules work, Crew SC would only keep 75 percent of the transfer fee for Steffen, or in this case $2.9 million. Of that, head coach and sporting director Gregg Berhalter can use roughly $750,000 as General Allocation Money and the remaining money can be used for investment in the club (towards a Designated Player or to improve training facilities, for example).
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   "Unless Berhalter and his staff believe Kempin is the present and second-year goalkeeper Logan Ketterer or rookie Ben Lundgaard are the future of the club, that would mean going out and signing another keeper in the near future. It would also mean that the rest of the money for the club would have to actually be reinvested, which — given the current possibility of relocation — seems unlikely."
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Therefore, because of Major League Soccer's Godfather system where Major League Soccer/Don Garber
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: medium;">
                   (fittingly
                  </span>
                  @thesoccerdon on twitter)
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   gets a little of everything that is one main reason why the Columbus Crew and Sporting Director/Manager Gregg Berhalter couldn't say "yes."
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Berhalter tries to do what is best for Crew players, even when it's difficult for Columbus, most of the time
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: medium;">
                   (see Justin Meram or Ola Kamara in recent history)
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   ; yet there is no reason a bidding war for US soccer's next big keeper would be a bad thing for the Columbus Crew and even Zack Steffen.
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   If $3.9 million is acceptable, there is no reason why $7.8 million couldn't be more acceptable.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Columbus went back to the drawing board multiple times
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   themselves
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   in their own offers for Milton Valenzuela and for others that didn't occur such as Jhon Murillo, Lucas Gamba.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Bristol City, who currently has Max O'Leary (who was on loan as keeper at Solihull Moors in the English 5th Division last season) and Frank Fielding (currently injured and who isn't likely a number one that can propel them to Premier League level anyways) probably foresaw a first offer being rejected.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Bristol City also has Niki Maenpaa, but the 33 year old Finnish keeper has only made 11 appearances with the club since 2015.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   With two weeks until their English Championship season begins the Robins therefore may have a second offer for Zack Steffen in them.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   However, even if Bristol City does gain Steffen's signature eventually, the club may still have to loan Zack to Columbus for the rest of the 2018 season
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: medium;">
                   (or loan him somewhere else)
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   until they can gain a work permit for him.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-lang="en">
                   <div dir="ltr" lang="en">
                    As I wrote in my initial story, something to keep in mind if Crew, Bristol and Steffen agree to deal: It'll be very hard for him to get an English work permit.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                    If the transfer goes through, there's potential he'll be loaned by Bristol (perhaps to Crew) until he can get a permit.
                   </div>
                   — Sam Stejskal (@samstejskal)
                   <a href="https://twitter.com/samstejskal/status/1019978934056833025?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                    July 19, 2018
                   </a>
                  </blockquote>
                  <script async="" charset="utf-8" src="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js">
                  </script>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   More here on the work permit issues from
                   <a href="https://bristolcity.vitalfootball.co.uk/former-brighton-player-on-trial-work-permit-issues-for-goalkeeper-this-deserves-a-round-up/">
                    Vital Football Bristol City
                   </a>
                   .
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Nevertheless, I'm guessing the Robins have completed their hedonistic calculus before making any offer to the Crew.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Bristol City likely doesn't figure it will be complicated to eventually win an appeal on a work permit for Steffen as the Crew keeper appears on track to be the sole benefactor, participant in the majority of goalkeeper caps for the United States in the next two years.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   I doubt likely works for the English courts though, but who knows.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Regardless of what Bristol City does...
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   I'm beginning to think Berhalter foreseen this in his looking glass in the future.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   As was personally a bit perplexed on draft day when Columbus selected Ben Lundgaard as our third goalkeeper behind Zack Steffen.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Was in the building and thought "why? what's the point of that as a number one pick?" as no one is starting over Steffen.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: medium;">
                   <i>
                    Lundgaard was a nice guy though.
                   </i>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                   <tbody>
                    <tr>
                     <td style="text-align: center;">
                      <a href="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-MzvL_-D42kM/W1HG72PJCSI/AAAAAAAAGSU/zWdbKkjUx7o7TWzr_m5y4-fmmG0_BwYbwCLcBGAs/s1600/Screenshot_20180720-072128.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                       <img border="0" data-original-height="1067" data-original-width="1078" height="316" src="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-MzvL_-D42kM/W1HG72PJCSI/AAAAAAAAGSU/zWdbKkjUx7o7TWzr_m5y4-fmmG0_BwYbwCLcBGAs/s320/Screenshot_20180720-072128.jpg" width="320"/>
                      </a>
                     </td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr>
                     <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </td>
                    </tr>
                   </tbody>
                  </table>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Well now makes a bit more sense.
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <script type="text/javascript">
                  createSummaryAndThumb("summary2718390232636884110");
                 </script>

           <div class="date-outer">
            <h2 class="date-header">
             <span>
              Wednesday, July 11, 2018
             </span>
            </h2>
            <div class="date-posts">
             <div class="post-outer">
              <div class="wrapfullpost">
               <div class="post hentry">
                <a name="2448974577225380529">
                </a>
                <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                 <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/07/patrick-mullins-bolsters-columbus-crew.html">
                  Patrick Mullins bolsters Columbus Crew forward line.
                 </a>
                </h3>
                <div class="post-header-line-1">
                </div>
                <div class="postmeta-primary">
                 <span class="meta_date">
                  8:19 PM
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_categories">
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_comments">
                  <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/07/patrick-mullins-bolsters-columbus-crew.html#comment-form" onclick="">
                   No comments
                  </a>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="post-body entry-content">
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <div id="summary2448974577225380529">
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                   <a href="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-yrxFPFUKb7s/W0a87R8BoiI/AAAAAAAAGSE/CHiOYrnOi-M5o_-TBVbfqr28kG_c738XQCLcBGAs/s1600/maryland.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                    <img border="0" data-original-height="342" data-original-width="1224" height="178" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-yrxFPFUKb7s/W0a87R8BoiI/AAAAAAAAGSE/CHiOYrnOi-M5o_-TBVbfqr28kG_c738XQCLcBGAs/s640/maryland.png" width="640"/>
                   </a>
                  </div>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   With Wayne Rooney and Darren Mattocks now in the D.C. United forward line, United had limited appearance time left for Patrick Mullins.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   As a result Columbus came in today with $150,000 targeted allocation money to acquire Patrick Mullins to hopefully improve their attacking options.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   In addition, Mullins will notice a few friendly faces in Columbus.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-lang="en">
                   <div dir="ltr" lang="en">
                    Welcome to Columbus, old friend 😉 let’s get to work
                    <a href="https://twitter.com/hashtag/terpfam?src=hash&amp;ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                     #terpfam
                    </a>
                    <a href="https://twitter.com/MarylandMSoccer?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                     @MarylandMSoccer
                    </a>
                    <a href="https://twitter.com/zackstef_23?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                     @zackstef_23
                    </a>
                    <a href="https://t.co/xdwVuKpBFJ">
                     https://t.co/xdwVuKpBFJ
                    </a>
                   </div>
                   — Alex Crognale (@alexcrognale)
                   <a href="https://twitter.com/alexcrognale/status/1017130529664036869?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                    July 11, 2018
                   </a>
                  </blockquote>
                  <script async="" charset="utf-8" src="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js">
                  </script>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   He'll join former Maryland college teammates Zack Steffen and Alex Crognale on the Columbus Crew.
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   Prior to this latest chapter commencing, Mullins had 13 goals for United in 44 appearances.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    In a heartfelt message,
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   D.C. general manager Dave Kasper commented that trading Mullins "
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   will provide us with assets and flexibility for future moves.
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   We wish Mullins the best in Columbus and thank him for his service to the club."
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   Columbus has to be a bit more creative compared to about every other team as they're never bringing in a Wayne Rooney.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   Therefore, improve where you can improve.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   For one, Mullins is a two time Hermann Trophy winner for best collegiate player. That doesn't just happen for being okay.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   For two, Mullins 23 goals in 96 overall MLS appearances is good for about a goal every fourth appearance.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   For three, sometimes he could pull off some gaga stuff.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <iframe allow="autoplay; encrypted-media" allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="315" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/KrfS6mGAxhg" width="560">
                  </iframe>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   Whereas, the Crew's current second striker Adam Jahn's 12 in 103 is good for a goal every eighth or ninth appearance.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   So a second option that may score in general would be nice.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   Further, for the most part, Gregg Berhalter has luck rehabilitating or putting strikers careers in extra boost mode in Columbus.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   "Patrick is a proven goalscorer who is dangerous inside the box and has a solid track record in MLS in his first five seasons," said Berhalter.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   That track record may get even more solid under Berhalter.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Berhalter has three options for Mullins:
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: medium;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    1.) Second striker, late substitute for Zardes.
                   </span>
                   <i>
                    Boring
                   </i>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   2.) Switch to two strikers to see if it bolsters what has been a weak attack.
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: medium;">
                   <i>
                    But we never change how we play even if it means we will never win anything.
                   </i>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   3.) If Zardes is okay with it try him back on a wing and put Mullins up top as Mullins and Zardes on the field is better than Zardes with Argudo or Martinez.
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: medium;">
                   <i>
                    Could be onto something if Zardes believes he can score on the wing, be as useful there too. Good luck.
                   </i>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <script type="text/javascript">
                  createSummaryAndThumb("summary2448974577225380529");
                 </script>
                 <div class="readmore">
                  <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/07/patrick-mullins-bolsters-columbus-crew.html">
                   Read More
                  </a>

           <div class="date-outer">
            <h2 class="date-header">
             <span>
              Monday, July 9, 2018
             </span>
            </h2>
            <div class="date-posts">
             <div class="post-outer">
              <div class="wrapfullpost">
               <div class="post hentry">
                <a name="5191569980596526704">
                </a>
                <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                 <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/07/was-refereeing-substandard-and-slanted.html">
                  Was refereeing substandard and slanted in Columbus loss in LA?
                 </a>
                </h3>
                <div class="post-header-line-1">
                </div>
                <div class="postmeta-primary">
                 <span class="meta_date">
                  4:56 AM
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_categories">
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_comments">
                  <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/07/was-refereeing-substandard-and-slanted.html#comment-form" onclick="">
                   No comments
                  </a>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="post-body entry-content">
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <div id="summary5191569980596526704">
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                   <a href="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-RJFP5liUHTY/W0NDIB4at5I/AAAAAAAAGR4/NsFPLgtzgEoyAO9-9eTYprvBfROaxU4egCLcBGAs/s1600/zlatan.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                    <img border="0" data-original-height="415" data-original-width="752" height="352" src="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-RJFP5liUHTY/W0NDIB4at5I/AAAAAAAAGR4/NsFPLgtzgEoyAO9-9eTYprvBfROaxU4egCLcBGAs/s640/zlatan.png" width="640"/>
                   </a>
                  </div>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   The central referee for the Los Angeles Galaxy vs. Columbus Crew match was supposed to be Hilaro Grajeda.
                  </span>
                  <a href="https://matchcenter.mlssoccer.com/matchcenter/2018-07-07-la-galaxy-vs-columbus-crew-sc/preview" style="font-size: x-large;">
                   Link
                  </a>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   .
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <img alt="Image result for Hilario Grajeda" height="266" src="https://cdn.vox-cdn.com/thumbor/GEmx3bFOvQV1yakWbSbD81lfHiw=/0x173:2499x1839/1200x800/filters:focal(0x173:2499x1839)/cdn.vox-cdn.com/uploads/chorus_image/image/49355623/usa-today-8136600.0.jpg" width="400"/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Instead the Columbus Crew on Saturday
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   received 30 year old Joseph Dickerson making his
                   <a href="http://cornerofthegalaxy.com/2018/07/08/la-galaxy-rumble-over-columbus-crew-with-four-goal-shutout/">
                    debut at center ref
                   </a>
                   .
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <img alt="Image result for Joseph Dickerson referee" height="356" src="http://proreferees.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/05/JosephDickerson-800x445-copy.jpg" width="640"/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   In parts, the debut was a bit of a head scratcher.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-lang="en">
                   <div dir="ltr" lang="en">
                    MLS Referee Rule Book Lessons. Lesson 84. How to referee a game in favor of a superstar and push the game in a positive direction for a rather lackluster team.
                    <a href="https://t.co/wO2fwnYdqI">
                     pic.twitter.com/wO2fwnYdqI
                    </a>
                   </div>
                   — CREWTURE.NET (@crewture)
                   <a href="https://twitter.com/crewture/status/1015825218500284416?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                    July 8, 2018
                   </a>
                  </blockquote>
                  <script async="" charset="utf-8" src="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js">
                  </script>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   Regardless, Columbus should've played better and put the game away well before LA's goal and the VAR overturn.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   Columbus needs to pick four every day starters in defense and just go with them.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   P
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   erhaps the same at other positions, as I think the
                   <i>
                    by committee
                   </i>
                   method is perhaps why Berhalter teams haven't broken through.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   Should know your best eleven by this point in the MLS season.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   But, at the very least Zlatan Ibrahimovic should've received a yellow on his retaliation hit on Lalas Abubukar.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   And it just gets more questionable from there.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Easy to blame it all on the referee though.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Columbus should be at a point in these games where they don't have to depend on referee calls and no calls.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-lang="en">
                   <div dir="ltr" lang="en">
                    I'm a bit tired of us controlling entire games and the other team scores. This Galaxy team is shit.
                   </div>
                   — CREWTURE.NET (@crewture)
                   <a href="https://twitter.com/crewture/status/1015798285108416512?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                    July 8, 2018
                   </a>
                  </blockquote>
                  <script async="" charset="utf-8" src="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js">
                  </script>
                  <br/>
                  <blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-lang="en">
                   <div dir="ltr" lang="en">
                    Whining over a call/no-call doesn’t cover up the fact that the Crew couldn’t score... that’s the real truth in why they lost
                   </div>
                   — Matt Ramah (@squathard)
                   <a href="https://twitter.com/squathard/status/1015950635999596544?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                    July 8, 2018
                   </a>
                  </blockquote>
                  <script async="" charset="utf-8" src="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js">
                  </script>

           <div class="date-outer">
            <h2 class="date-header">
             <span>
              Thursday, July 5, 2018
             </span>
            </h2>
            <div class="date-posts">
             <div class="post-outer">
              <div class="wrapfullpost">
               <div class="post hentry">
                <a name="2836623863842696546">
                </a>
                <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                 <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/07/game-preview-who-can-reach-higher.html">
                  GAME PREVIEW: Who can reach higher heights after their former Major League Soccer career club.
                 </a>
                </h3>
                <div class="post-header-line-1">
                </div>
                <div class="postmeta-primary">
                 <span class="meta_date">
                  9:39 PM
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_categories">
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_comments">
                  <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/07/game-preview-who-can-reach-higher.html#comment-form" onclick="">
                   No comments
                  </a>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="post-body entry-content">
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <div id="summary2836623863842696546">
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                   <a href="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Rv7RaeXS8jY/Wz7g-lDj7oI/AAAAAAAAGQs/-mgLHalS-MoYUmY5UZpZtCT8SiREzepNwCLcBGAs/s1600/gyasiola.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                    <img border="0" data-original-height="362" data-original-width="1294" height="178" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Rv7RaeXS8jY/Wz7g-lDj7oI/AAAAAAAAGQs/-mgLHalS-MoYUmY5UZpZtCT8SiREzepNwCLcBGAs/s640/gyasiola.png" width="640"/>
                   </a>
                  </div>
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                  </div>
                  <br/>
                  <b style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <b style="font-family: inherit;">
                    <b style="font-family: inherit;">
                     <br/>
                    </b>
                   </b>
                  </b>
                  <b style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <b style="font-family: inherit;">
                    <b style="font-family: inherit;">
                     Columbus Crew (8-5-6) - 30 points- Fourth place in the East @
                    </b>
                    LA Galaxy (6-7-4) - 22 points- Eighth place in the West
                   </b>
                  </b>
                  <br/>
                  <div>
                   <div style="font-size: medium; text-align: start;">
                    <b style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                     <br/>
                    </b>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      For over five years, his entire pro career prior to coming to Columbus, Gyasi Zardes was a LA Galaxy player. For 1,857 days.
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <br/>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      <br/>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      Zardes was signed by LA on December 20th, 2012 and left on
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                     January 20th, 2018.
                    </span>
                    <br/>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      <br/>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      In comparison, Ola Kamara's span with Columbus doesn't reach half of that.
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <br/>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      <br/>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      Ola was black and gold from February 4th, 2016 to January 20th, 2018 o
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                     r 716 days.
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      <br/>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      What I find particularly interesting are both strikers with and without Berhalter.
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <br/>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      <br/>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <img alt="Related image" height="137" src="https://league-mp7static.mlsdigital.net/styles/image_landscape/s3/images/Berhalter.jpg?null&amp;itok=bNBsLYVy&amp;c=08ce797bb0b111f4ccfb5e64e152df15" width="320"/>
                    <br/>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      Ola Kamara: 34 goals in 59 games
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <br/>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      <br/>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <img alt="Image result for berhalter zardes" src="https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcQp6XUmZgmQmO4wASZYrj0ZyEAzHC9SI5Nqwgz0CfCbW62sCoz3"/>
                    <br/>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     Gyasi Zardes: 11 goals in 19 games
                    </span>
                    <br/>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <br/>
                    </span>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     And without 3G's magic touch...
                    </span>
                    <br/>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <br/>
                    </span>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     Ola Kamara: 70 goals in 208 games
                    </span>
                    <br/>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <br/>
                    </span>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     Gyasi Zardes: 34 goals in 131 games
                    </span>
                    <i>
                     some at fullback.
                    </i>
                    <br/>
                    <i>
                     <br/>
                    </i>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     I think both strikers will have something to prove on Saturday.
                    </span>
                    <br/>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <br/>
                    </span>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     For Ola, that he can do this at other places than Columbus.
                    </span>
                    <br/>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <br/>
                    </span>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     For Gyasi, that LA made a huge mistake in utilizing him.
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div style="font-size: medium; text-align: start;">
                    <br/>
                   </div>
                   <div style="font-size: medium; text-align: start;">
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                     <b>
                      Crewture's projected Crew lineup:
                     </b>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div>
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                     <b>
                      <br/>
                     </b>
                    </span>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     Just let Federico stay home and rest on Saturday.
                    </span>
                    <br/>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <br/>
                    </span>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     Especially if Sosa has a few more goals in him, see where that streak goes.
                    </span>
                    <br/>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <br/>
                    </span>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     In general would keep the roster about the same, see if roster familarity for once can get some wins going again.
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div style="font-size: medium; text-align: start;">
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <br/>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div class="separator" style="clear: both; font-size: medium;">
                   </div>
                   <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                    <a href="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-3hAmQj2Js_Q/Wz7sGAFmilI/AAAAAAAAGQ8/2Jg6lwjfR68_0Xa6lFzd5rHibs4DEGbRQCLcBGAs/s1600/lacrew.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                     <img border="0" data-original-height="788" data-original-width="1260" height="400" src="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-3hAmQj2Js_Q/Wz7sGAFmilI/AAAAAAAAGQ8/2Jg6lwjfR68_0Xa6lFzd5rHibs4DEGbRQCLcBGAs/s640/lacrew.png" width="640"/>
                    </a>
                   </div>
                   <div class="separator" style="clear: both; font-size: medium;">
                    <br/>
                   </div>
                   <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     With Steffen out again lets hope Kempin gets motivated as well
                    </span>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     against his former team.
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <br/>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     Would give Ketterer a chance or two but that's just me.
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <br/>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     A win in LA on Saturday would convince me otherwise.
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div style="font-size: medium; text-align: start;">
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                     <b>
                      <br/>
                     </b>
                    </span>
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                     <b>
                      LA Galaxy projected lineup:
                     </b>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div>
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                     <b>
                      <br/>
                     </b>
                    </span>
                    <span style="color: #1b2226; font-size: large;">
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      Ola Kamara is questionable with a calf injury..
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <br/>
                    <span style="color: #1b2226; font-size: large;">
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      <br/>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span style="color: #1b2226; font-size: large;">
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      Yet feel like Kamara will find a way to get on the field against his former club.
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <br/>
                    <span style="color: #1b2226; font-size: large;">
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      <br/>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span style="color: #1b2226; font-size: large;">
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      I think LA will shoot for a lineup somewhat like this.
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div style="font-size: medium; text-align: start;">
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                     <span style="background-color: white; color: #1b2226;">
                      <br/>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                    <a href="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-lRzvdqtx-vc/Wz7ukWI5GcI/AAAAAAAAGRI/_vAWUOCjrMk1i98xJ09mb5UXQe5nfp9ygCLcBGAs/s1600/lateam.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                     <img border="0" data-original-height="336" data-original-width="449" height="298" src="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-lRzvdqtx-vc/Wz7ukWI5GcI/AAAAAAAAGRI/_vAWUOCjrMk1i98xJ09mb5UXQe5nfp9ygCLcBGAs/s400/lateam.png" width="400"/>
                    </a>
                   </div>
                   <div class="separator" style="clear: both; font-size: medium;">
                    <br/>
                   </div>
                   <div>
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     It's funny that LA utilized Gyasi as a fullback and now utilizes Ola as a midfielder.
                    </span>
                    <br/>
                    <div style="font-size: medium;">
                     <br/>
                    </div>
                   </div>
                   <div style="font-size: medium; text-align: start;">
                    <b style="font-size: x-large; text-align: center;">
                     PREDICTION:
                     <span style='font-family: "times new roman";'>
                      2-1 Columbus. Brace by Zardes, Ibrahimovic on the other end.
                     </span>
                    </b>
                    <br/>
                    <b style="font-size: x-large; text-align: center;">
                     <span style='font-family: "times new roman";'>
                      <br/>
                     </span>
                    </b>
                    <br/>
                    <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                    </div>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>

            <h2 class="date-header">
             <span>
              Friday, June 22, 2018
             </span>
            </h2>
            <div class="date-posts">
             <div class="post-outer">
              <div class="wrapfullpost">
               <div class="post hentry">
                <a name="6647114332210172570">
                </a>
                <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                 <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/06/tyson-wahls-opinion-is-very-small.html">
                  In any Columbus Crew locker room, Tyson Wahl's opinion is a very small one.
                 </a>
                </h3>
                <div class="post-header-line-1">
                </div>
                <div class="postmeta-primary">
                 <span class="meta_date">
                  11:38 AM
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_categories">
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_comments">
                  <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/06/tyson-wahls-opinion-is-very-small.html#comment-form" onclick="">
                   No comments
                  </a>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="post-body entry-content">
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <div id="summary6647114332210172570">
                  <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                   <tbody>
                    <tr>
                     <td style="text-align: center;">
                      <a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-h0QkY7PKHhE/Wy03ikMWGOI/AAAAAAAAGP8/ENvxQB0sEIE_bnYTKH0tK_OxtQolbpjegCLcBGAs/s1600/20180309_205331.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                       <img border="0" data-original-height="1200" data-original-width="1600" height="480" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-h0QkY7PKHhE/Wy03ikMWGOI/AAAAAAAAGP8/ENvxQB0sEIE_bnYTKH0tK_OxtQolbpjegCLcBGAs/s640/20180309_205331.jpg" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr>
                     <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                       <br/>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div style="text-align: left;">
                       <span style="font-size: large;">
                        At the start of the season, former Crew players Alejandro Moreno, Gino Padula, Andy Greunebaum, Steven Lenhart, Jason Garey, Dante Washington, and Andy Iro came back to share pro-SaveTheCrew opinions.
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <span style="font-size: large;">
                      </span>
                     </td>
                    </tr>
                   </tbody>
                  </table>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                   So it was strange when a week ago one former Columbus Crew player went way off the wall.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   As center back Tyson Wahl now lives in Austin, Texas and apparently supports Precourt Sports Ventures moving the Columbus Crew to Austin and McKalla place.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-lang="en">
                   <div dir="ltr" lang="en">
                    RT from mls2atx "Ten days until
                    <a href="https://twitter.com/hashtag/ATXCouncil?src=hash&amp;ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                     #ATXCouncil
                    </a>
                    . The support is there. The time is now. Let's bring
                    <a href="https://twitter.com/hashtag/MLS2ATX?src=hash&amp;ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                     #MLS2ATX
                    </a>
                    .
                    <a href="https://t.co/TQhJqE1EIA">
                     pic.twitter.com/TQhJqE1EIA
                    </a>
                    "
                   </div>
                   — Eye on Austin (@EyeonAustin)
                   <a href="https://twitter.com/EyeonAustin/status/1008742934769033216?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                    June 18, 2018
                   </a>
                  </blockquote>
                  <script async="" charset="utf-8" src="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js">
                  </script>
                  <br/>
                  <div style="background-color: white; margin-bottom: 1em;">
                   <div style="color: #1d2129;">
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                     Then he tried to
                     <a href="https://www.prosoccerusa.com/mls/columbus-crew-sc/former-crew-sc-player-tyson-wahl-discusses-his-support-for-the-mls2atx-campaign/">
                      defend his comments and reasoning to Pro Soccer USA
                     </a>
                     (sort of).
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div style="color: #1d2129;">
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                     <br/>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div style="border: 0px; line-height: 1.5; margin-bottom: 15px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                    <div style="color: #444444;">
                     <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                      “I have super fond memories of my time in Columbus. I had a great time there and I loved playing for that team. I really enjoyed my four years there. I think the [#SavetheCrew campaign] is the natural thing that a group of fans would do in this scenario. I follow the Crew closely. I support the team and those players…I wish them all good luck, as I do many players across the league.”
                     </span>
                    </div>
                    <div style="color: #444444;">
                     <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                      <br/>
                     </span>
                    </div>
                    <span style="color: #444444; font-size: large;">
                     Cool.
                    </span>
                    <span style="color: #444444; font-size: large;">
                     🙄
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div style="border: 0px; color: #444444; line-height: 1.5; margin-bottom: 15px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                     “Obviously, I’ve been following this season. I’ve been following the story the whole time. I know there would be a group of fans that wouldn’t be too happy to see that,” Wahl said, “I just think that Austin is a great city and MLS can do very well in this city. With other clubs around the country right now, like the Atlantas and the Orlandos, doing so well in their cities, the standard has really risen. Austin can have that type of support.”
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div style="color: #1d2129;">
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                     <br/>
                    </span>
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                     On a short list of not the best Crew center backs, I guess Wahl wasn't too worried about keeping up his image in Columbus.
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div style="color: #1d2129;">
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                     <br/>
                    </span>
                    <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                     Nevertheless, one lackey aside when the #SaveTheCrew Battle For Columbus Documentary came out in Columbus to start the season several former Crew players were there sharing better opinions.
                    </span>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <div style="background-color: white; color: #1d2129; margin-bottom: 1em;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    Made a following new video with
                    <a class="_58cn" data-ft='{"tn":"*N","type":104}' href="https://www.facebook.com/hashtag/savethecrew?source=feed_text" style="color: #365899; cursor: pointer; text-decoration-line: none;">
                     <span class="_5afx" style="direction: ltr; unicode-bidi: isolate;">
                      <span aria-label="hashtag" class="_58cl _5afz" style="unicode-bidi: isolate;">
                       #
                      </span>
                      <span class="_58cm">
                       SaveTheCrew
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </a>
                    commentary from Gino Padula and Steven Lenhart.
                   </span>
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                   <br/>
                   <blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-lang="en">
                    <div dir="ltr" lang="en">
                     Following video with
                     <a href="https://twitter.com/hashtag/SaveTheCrew?src=hash&amp;ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                      #SaveTheCrew
                     </a>
                     commentary from Gino Padula and Steven Lenhart so you can take your cutesy little Tyson Wahl comments and stick them you know where
                     <a href="https://twitter.com/APrecourt?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                      @APrecourt
                     </a>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     And just so you know we never back down.
                     <a href="https://t.co/ZmY1OwFRra">
                      pic.twitter.com/ZmY1OwFRra
                     </a>
                    </div>
                    — CREWTURE.NET (@crewture)
                    <a href="https://twitter.com/crewture/status/1010210189109276672?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                     June 22, 2018
                    </a>
                   </blockquote>
                   <span style="background-color: transparent; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                   <span style="background-color: transparent; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    Nearly all former Crew players thoughts from that night.
                   </span>
                  </div>
                  <br/>
                  <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="360" mozallowfullscreen="" src="https://player.vimeo.com/video/276556943" webkitallowfullscreen="" width="640">
