           <div class="date-outer">
            <h2 class="date-header">
             <span>
              Tuesday, June 19, 2018
             </span>
            </h2>
            <div class="date-posts">
             <div class="post-outer">
              <div class="wrapfullpost">
               <div class="post hentry">
                <a name="3168911979769606838">
                </a>
                <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                 <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/06/the-venezuelan-jhon-murillo-back-in-as.html">
                  The Venezuelan Jhon Murillo back in as a Crew target?
                 </a>
                </h3>
                <div class="post-header-line-1">
                </div>
                <div class="postmeta-primary">
                 <span class="meta_date">
                  9:08 PM
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_categories">
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_comments">
                  <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/06/the-venezuelan-jhon-murillo-back-in-as.html#comment-form" onclick="">
                   No comments
                  </a>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="post-body entry-content">
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <div id="summary3168911979769606838">
                  <img alt="Image result for Jhon Murillo" src="https://alchetron.com/cdn/jhon-murillo-564266f6-f7a0-471f-96e9-ef9ea9f66b4-resize-750.jpeg"/>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   For the second Summer in a row it appears likely that the 22-year-old Venezuelan Jhon Murillo is again a Crew target. A Bola
                   <a href="https://www.abola.pt/nnh/Noticias/Ver/736041">
                    link
                   </a>
                   and ZeroZero.pt
                   <a href="https://translate.google.com/translate?sl=auto&amp;tl=en&amp;js=y&amp;prev=_t&amp;hl=en&amp;ie=UTF-8&amp;u=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.zerozero.pt%2Fnews.php%3Fid%3D223876&amp;edit-text=&amp;act=url">
                    link
                   </a>
                   .
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   The Columbus Crew offered Benfica $2.5 million to $3.1 million for the striker/winger last July.
                   <a href="http://www.record.pt/futebol/futebol-nacional/liga-nos/benfica/detalhe/jhon-murillo-perto-de-rumar-ao-columbus-crew.html">
                    LINK
                   </a>
                   .
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   The first reports came across on July 5th, 2017 (
                   <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2017/07/gshs-for-75-let-silly-season-begin-crew.html">
                    LINK
                   </a>
                   ). Columbus wanted to buy Murillo outright whereas Benfica wanted to just put the talent on loan.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   The two clubs went back and forth most of July 2017 before Benfica loaned Murillo to Turkish Super Lig side Kasimpasa on July 29th, 2017.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   Benfica wanted more for a full on transfer.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   Murillo made 25 appearances and scored 5 goals for Kasimpasa since then but returns to Benfica still not a part of their plans.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   Benfica still appears to want more.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: medium;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Murillo has a few other current possible suitors in Portuguese clubs Braga and Tondela. Murillo was on loan with Tondela prior to Kasimpasa yet neither Portuguese minnow
                   </span>
                   (i
                   <i>
                    n comparison to Benfica)
                   </i>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    can likely offer the $3 million plus that Benfica requires.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: medium;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: medium;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Major League Soccer may step up to the plate this time.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: medium;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: medium;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    If Murillo turns out to be even half of what another Venezuelan, one Josef Martinez has been in this league it would be worthwhile.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   Berhalter had his hat in the ring last Summer for Murillo and is still looking for the same position again; as d
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   espite having more winger options than striker options,
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   Berhalter can never seem to have enough wingers.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   Appears Berhalter believes he needs a winger on the other side of Pedro Santos at either the Jhon Murillo or
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    Przemysław
                   </span>
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    Frankowski
                   </span>
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    level compared to the Hansen, Martinez level.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    Cannot hurt.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    Columbus's last game at home against Atlanta shows they are definitely not at the Major League Soccer mountain top yet.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <iframe allow="autoplay; encrypted-media" allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="315" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/5sov_dtwzBg" width="560">
                  </iframe>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <script type="text/javascript">
                  createSummaryAndThumb("summary3168911979769606838");
                 </script>

                  GAME PREVIEW: Golden Boot showdown
                 </a>
                </h3>

                </div>
                <div class="postmeta-primary">
                 <span class="meta_date">
                  12:38 PM

                     <td style="text-align: center;">
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">

                        <img border="0" data-original-height="500" data-original-width="686" height="466" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-LXQLhs3nvaI/WyAibxfLJsI/AAAAAAAAGPk/zoNBIWOSET8A7BgQxP4F3T4w3U-T-X-TwCLcBGAs/s640/goldenboot.png" width="640"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                     </td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr>
                     <td class="tr-caption" style="font-size: 12.8px;">
                      <span style="font-size: small;">
                       Number 1 on the goal scoring chart Josef Martinez (13 tallies) goes up against number 2 on that list in Gyasi Zardes (10 tallies) this Wednesday
                      </span>
                     </td>
                    </tr>
                   </tbody>
                  </table>
                  <br/>
                  <b style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <b style="font-family: inherit;">
                    <b style="font-family: inherit;">
                     Atlanta United (9-3-3) - 30 points- First place in the East @
                    </b>
                    Columbus Crew (7-3-6) - 27 points- Third place in the East
                   </b>
                  </b>
                  <br/>
                  <b style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </b>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    The huge games for the Columbus Crew refuse to slow down
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   as of late
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   .
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    Columbus faces off against the first place team in the East, the first place team in the entire league in Atlanta United this Wednesday at home.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    Columbus has nine games without a defeat but needs to stop another not as glimmering recent trend.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    Ties at home.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    The trend started off swell enough as a 3-0 sure defeat turned into a 3-3 tie at home against Toronto FC.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    However, the trend has been compacted by a 2-2 tie to Chicago that led to U.S. Open Cup elimination.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    Then the trend became a bit tiresome against New York Red Bull.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    That competition ended in a 1-1 tie, but was a game where a 3-0 or 4-0 lead for Columbus by the end of the first half would've been more deserving.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    If Columbus could've finished some rather typical conversions in that game the Crew would've found themselves with an opportunity to take first place for themselves on Wednesday.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-lang="en">
                   <div dir="ltr" lang="en">
                    The moment yesterday when you know the game is going to end up at the most as a tie.
                    <br/>
                    <br/>

                    June 10, 2018
                   </a>

                  <script async="" charset="utf-8" src="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js">
                  </script>

                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    Nevertheless, if you overlook Atlanta's one game in hand,
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   the Crew can still tie for first.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   Perhaps more importantly Columbus can put some distance between themselves and the rest of the Eastern Conference.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white;">
                    Always with games in hand.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <b>
                    Crewture's projected Crew lineup:
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <b>
                    <br/>
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   What will help turn the tide for Columbus at home is the return of Zack Steffen.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   In addition, the return of both Pedro Santos and Wil Trapp (even if
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Ricardo Clark is about a zero percent drop off in most respects)
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   won't hurt
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   .
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                  </div>
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                   <a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-rSNRNfJrNWs/WyAY-ISQGwI/AAAAAAAAGPE/zUjSnRlYnO8sofSxeCC24TH9YiOd6ROMACLcBGAs/s1600/atlanta%2B%25281%2529.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                    <img border="0" data-original-height="788" data-original-width="1260" height="400" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-rSNRNfJrNWs/WyAY-ISQGwI/AAAAAAAAGPE/zUjSnRlYnO8sofSxeCC24TH9YiOd6ROMACLcBGAs/s640/atlanta%2B%25281%2529.png" width="640"/>
                   </a>
                  </div>
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                   <br/>
                  </div>
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Another lineup question to ponder is whether Eduardo Sosa plays a role again at some point?
                   </span>
                  </div>
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </div>
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Other than Crognale's goal, Sosa was the most vital substitute out of the three to turn a sure defeat into a tie against Toronto FC.
                   </span>
                  </div>
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </div>
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    He looked good again against New York Red Bull:
                   </span>
                  </div>
                  <blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-lang="en">

                    June 10, 2018
                   </a>
                  </blockquote>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Has been a huge bright spot as looks like Berhalter is onto something with Sosa compared to the
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   Steindórsson's and Larsen's of the world.
                  </span>
                  <br/>

                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">

                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white; color: #1b2226;">
                    Atlanta United trotted out the following lineup in a 1-1 tie at NYCFC the last game out:
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white; color: #1b2226;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>

                   </a>

                   <div style="text-align: left;">
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     Atlanta was fortunate as Brad Guzan had to make nine saves to give Atlanta United a point.
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div style="text-align: left;">
                    <span style="font-size: large;">
                     <br/>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div style="text-align: left;">
                    <span style="background-color: white;">
                     <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                      “Tough and unfair, I think it’s probably the first point we’ve taken without deserving it,” Tata Martino said. “New York was the better team in the second half. Up until Josef’s goal, the game was fairly even. But after that New York was the better team.”
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div style="text-align: left;">
                    <span style="background-color: white;">
                     <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                      <br/>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div style="text-align: left;">
                    <span style="background-color: white;">
                     <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                      Even without Zack Steffen this past week, overall Columbus has been better in comparison to Atlanta United as of late.
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div style="text-align: left;">
                    <span style="background-color: white;">
                     <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                      <br/>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div style="text-align: left;">
                    <span style="background-color: white;">
                     <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                      Grabbing twelve out of the last eighteen possible points compared to Atlanta's eight.
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div style="text-align: left;">
                    <span style="background-color: white;">
                     <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                      <br/>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                   <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                    <a href="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-NtIq7bFHbYw/WyAe6-LEScI/AAAAAAAAGPY/KgY462HJfAIUed4IGqDCyHVrjgmZHOHBgCEwYBhgL/s1600/atlanta2.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                     <img border="0" data-original-height="106" data-original-width="326" height="104" src="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-NtIq7bFHbYw/WyAe6-LEScI/AAAAAAAAGPY/KgY462HJfAIUed4IGqDCyHVrjgmZHOHBgCEwYBhgL/s320/atlanta2.png" width="320"/>

                    <span style="background-color: white;">
                     <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                      If Columbus make it fifteen out of twenty-one possible compared to Atlanta's eight out of twenty-one possible, Columbus puts themselves in a good place to eventually not just tie for first but take it for themselves.
                     </span>
                    </span>

                <a name="2180580456125532132">
                </a>
                <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                 <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/06/game-preview-columbus-needs-to-get-back.html">
                  GAME PREVIEW: Columbus needs to get back on track before a new habit begins
                 </a>
                </h3>
                <div class="post-header-line-1">
                </div>
                <div class="postmeta-primary">
                 <span class="meta_date">
                  7:38 PM
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_categories">
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_comments">
                  <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/06/game-preview-columbus-needs-to-get-back.html#comment-form" onclick="">
                   No comments
                  </a>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="post-body entry-content">
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <div id="summary2180580456125532132">
                  <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                   <tbody>
                    <tr>
                     <td style="text-align: center;">
                      <a href="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-dLQUHUMrHF4/WxnpGOnhEsI/AAAAAAAAGOo/mP41TeO5Fa0OqIqIQ9RBBrC5UfwvF4WcQCLcBGAs/s1600/hejdukhejduk.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                       <img border="0" data-original-height="357" data-original-width="594" height="384" src="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-dLQUHUMrHF4/WxnpGOnhEsI/AAAAAAAAGOo/mP41TeO5Fa0OqIqIQ9RBBrC5UfwvF4WcQCLcBGAs/s640/hejdukhejduk.png" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr>
                     <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-size: small;">
                       Channel the Hejduk. Columbus needs to get back to three points at home against NYRB.
                      </span>
                     </td>
                    </tr>
                   </tbody>
                  </table>
                  <br/>
                  <b style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <b style="font-family: inherit;">
                    <b style="font-family: inherit;">
                     New York Red Bull (7-4-1) - 22 points- Fourth place in the East @
                    </b>
                    Columbus Crew (7-3-5) - 26 points- Third place in the East
                   </b>
                  </b>
                  <br/>
                  <b style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </b>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Columbus Crew has a huge game this weekend at home on ESPN.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    A win gives Columbus a possible seven point lead over the fourth, fifth, and sixth place teams in the East.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Some cushion would be a good thing at the moment.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    In addition, Columbus needs to nip in the bud what happened in the last two games at home.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    The comeback over Toronto F.C. w
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   as fun and entertaining.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   Looking at the first 67 minutes could've ended up A LOT worse.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   Nevertheless, it's still only a point at home.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   Have to get back to winning as quickly as you can because the rest of the East will catch up.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <b>
                    Crewture's projected Crew lineup:
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <b>
                    <br/>
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   It's cute that Berhalter, Major League Soccer in general is cool with releasing players to national teams for friendlies.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Since it isn't apparently as serious as all those big European leagues.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Was cool to see our shutout streak go by the wayside in a big way in the 3-3 tie to Toronto FC.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Especially when Steffen didn't even play against Ireland.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Him and Trapp will be gone again this weekend to hopefully see the field in France.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                  </div>
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                   <a href="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-j8vVWDfL4g8/WxnowE-AdOI/AAAAAAAAGOc/GNieLvC8JCY7KWrYiQLAVmEKHLsoGF8kACLcBGAs/s1600/myrb2.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                    <img border="0" data-original-height="788" data-original-width="1260" height="400" src="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-j8vVWDfL4g8/WxnowE-AdOI/AAAAAAAAGOc/GNieLvC8JCY7KWrYiQLAVmEKHLsoGF8kACLcBGAs/s640/myrb2.png" width="640"/>
                   </a>
                  </div>
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                   <br/>
                  </div>
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                   <br/>
                  </div>
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Cristian Martinez is still suspended.
                   </span>
                  </div>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Jonathan Mensah and Pedro Santos are questionable with injuries.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <b>
                    <br/>
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <b>
                    New York Red Bull projected lineup:
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <b>
                    <br/>
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white; color: #1b2226;">
                    New York Red Bulls last game out in Major League Soccer was a 2-1 defeat at New England.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: white; color: #1b2226;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                   <a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Ul9baafEtFI/WxnlBckQs5I/AAAAAAAAGOQ/cbMYP2tNdRcWYUszBLoHRuWxs725oga0gCLcBGAs/s1600/myrb1.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                    <img border="0" data-original-height="348" data-original-width="445" height="312" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Ul9baafEtFI/WxnlBckQs5I/AAAAAAAAGOQ/cbMYP2tNdRcWYUszBLoHRuWxs725oga0gCLcBGAs/s400/myrb1.png" width="400"/>
                   </a>
                  </div>
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                   <br/>
                  </div>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   If you wanted to complain about having Zack Steffen and Wil Trapp gone though look at who New York Red Bull has been without because of international friendly duty.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: #fafbfc; color: #1b2226;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    Just about half of their starting lineup. D - Fidel Escobar, D - Michael Murillo, D - Tim Parker, M - Tyler Adams, M - Kaku.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: #fafbfc; color: #1b2226;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: #fafbfc; color: #1b2226;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    Despite being a bit shorthanded NYRB had a much better U.S. Open Cup midweek showing then Columbus.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: #fafbfc; color: #1b2226;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: #fafbfc;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    <span style="color: #1b2226; font-family: inherit;">
                     NYRB demolished rivals NYCFC 4-0
                    </span>
                    <span style="color: #1b2226;">
                     resultantly
                    </span>
                    <span style="color: #1b2226; font-family: inherit;">
                     we'll see if that gets them in the mood here in Columbus.
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: #fafbfc; color: #1b2226;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: #fafbfc; color: #1b2226;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    Their expected lineup:
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <em style="background-color: #fafbfc; box-sizing: border-box; color: #1b2226;">
                    (4-2-3-1, right to left)
                   </em>
                   <br style="background-color: #fafbfc; box-sizing: border-box; color: #1b2226;"/>
                   <span style="background-color: #fafbfc; color: #1b2226;">
                    GK: Luis Robles — Connor Lade, Aaron Long, Aurelien Collin, Kemar Lawrence — Sean Davis, Marc Rzatkowski — Florian Valot, Vincent Bezecourt, Danny Royer — Bradley Wright-Phillips
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <div style="text-align: center;">
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </div>
                  <br/>
                  <b style="font-size: x-large; text-align: center;">
                   PREDICTION:
                   <span style='font-family: "times new roman";'>
                    3-2 Columbus.
                   </span>
                  </b>

                <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                 <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/06/romain-gall-receives-interest-from-sc.html">
                  Romain Gall receives interest from SC Heerenveen, Reserves to play in U.S. Open Cup, McKalla Place battle begins
                 </a>
                </h3>
                <div class="post-header-line-1">
                </div>
                <div class="postmeta-primary">
                 <span class="meta_date">
                  8:11 PM
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_categories">
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_comments">

                 </p>

                   <span style="color: yellow; font-size: large; text-align: center;">
                    <strong>
                     <a href="https://vimeo.com/174028056" onclick="window.open('https://vimeo.com/174028056','popup','width=900,height=600'); return false;" style='font-family: georgia, "times new roman", serif;' target="popup">

                    <img border="0" data-original-height="284" data-original-width="1600" height="112" src="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-gYiEmZy9Ue4/WxdQfML1M8I/AAAAAAAAGN4/e3eqC4UO2CMEkmAiioJzJc45vi-4p2AYgCLcBGAs/s640/65gsh.png" width="640"/>
                   </a>

                  <b style="font-family: inherit; font-size: x-large;">
                   <i>
                    Gaven..
                   </i>
                  </b>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <b>
                    Romain Gall receives interest from SC Heerenveen
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   With already one former Columbus Crew player in SC Heerenveen's roster in defender Nicolai Naess, SC Heerenveen could be after another former Crew player.
                   <a href="http://www.v-bal.nl/nieuws/298673/romain-gall-van-sundsvall-gescout-door-sc-heerenveen.html">
                    Link
                   </a>
                   .
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   SC Heerenveen is interested in attacker Romain Gall of the Swedish GIF Sundsvall, reports
                   <a href="https://www.fotbollskanalen.se/allsvenskan/hollandska-klubben-pa-plats-for-att-spana-in-gall-stammer/">
                    Fotbollskanalen
                   </a>
                   . In the middle of May SC Heerenveen scouts were at the game between Sundsvall and IF Brommapojkarna to see the 23-year-old right-wing attacker at work.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   There haven't been any other reports but SC Heerenveen would likely have to wait until July anyway to put in their transfer offer.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <iframe allow="autoplay; encrypted-media" allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="315" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/gM0gbhBU05Q" width="560">
                  </iframe>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <b style="font-family: inherit;">
                   <i>
                    <span style="font-size: x-large;">
                     Schelotto..
                    </span>
                   </i>
                  </b>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <b>
                    Berhalter will trot out reserves in US Open Cup tomorrow
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   The three players that turned around last Saturday's game (Crognale, Sosa, and Argudo) will likely be starting the U.S. Open Cup tomorrow.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Which may not be a bad thing as Columbus didn't decide to play until the three came in. Although the change in the result was 50% that and 50% formation change.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   And 50% Michael Bradley... 😅
                  </span>
                  <br/>

                  </div>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <span style="color: black; font-size: large; text-align: center;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <b style="font-family: inherit; font-size: x-large;">
                   <i>
                    Gaven..
                   </i>
                  </b>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <b>
                    Frankowski transfer update
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <b>
                    <br/>
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   A little bit of an update on the Frankowski to Major League Soccer with the Columbus Crew or Chicago Fire news.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: #f5f8fa; white-space: pre-wrap;">
                    Chicago/Columbus/MLS is willing to pay $1.7 million for Frankowski (link in Twitter article below). Jagiellonia Bialystok wants $2.5 million Euros though (nearly $3 million).
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: #f5f8fa; white-space: pre-wrap;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <span style="background-color: #f5f8fa; white-space: pre-wrap;">
                    There is also interest as well in Turkey from Bursaspor and Galatasaray. Nevertheless, Frankowski will likely stay in Poland according to reports and go to Polish champions Legia Warsaw.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <b>
                    <br/>
                   </b>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-lang="en">

                    <a href="https://t.co/GM8kaWmLjI">
                     https://t.co/GM8kaWmLjI

           <div class="date-outer">
            <h2 class="date-header">
             <span>
              Sunday, June 3, 2018
             </span>
            </h2>
            <div class="date-posts">
             <div class="post-outer">
              <div class="wrapfullpost">
               <div class="post hentry">
                <a name="1449496620062437541">
                </a>
                <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                 <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/06/never-quit.html">
                  Never Quit
                 </a>
                </h3>
                <div class="post-header-line-1">
                </div>
                <div class="postmeta-primary">
                 <span class="meta_date">
                  7:29 AM
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_categories">
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_comments">
                  <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/06/never-quit.html#comment-form" onclick="">
                   No comments
                  </a>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="post-body entry-content">
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 <div id="summary1449496620062437541">
                  <img src="https://pbs.twimg.com/media/DevLxNlUEAAPQ95.jpg:small"/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   66 minutes pass into a game and your down 3-0 at home.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   There were no quitters on that field last night in yellow.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Similar to Liverpool in the 2005 Champions League Final,  Columbus made up a 3-0 deficit.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   But even goal number one, two, and three in Liverpool's comeback in 2005 arrived before Columbus's first in the 67th minute last night.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   I felt like last night's contest symbolically, from beginning to end, could be linked
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   inextricably
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   to the #SaveTheCrew effort.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   The first 67 minutes are us in a nutshell.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   There is usually little to no hope when a rich owner decides it is time to pack up and leave a town.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Ask the Cleveland Browns, Seattle Supersonics, and Oakland Raiders.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Similarly, there is little to no hope when your down 3-0 in soccer with 25 minutes left.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   But Columbus never quits.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Fans started #SaveTheCrew.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Those fans have pro golfers wearing #SaveTheCrew hats.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Those fans invaded the College Gameday crowd.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   They'll try anything until the right person notices, listens.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                   Apparently Gregg Berhalter will try anything as well.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   In the 63rd minute he subbed in Eduardo Sosa for his first MLS regular season minutes, Alex Crognale for his second time for more than a few minutes at the end of a game, and Luis Argudo.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   3-0 down turned into a 3-3 final.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Eduardo Sosa played phenomenally well I thought. His performance was getting the opportunity and capitalizing.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Alex Crognale additionally says "hey don't forget about me" and grabbed the second goal.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style='background-color: white; color: #343434; font-family: "arial" , sans-serif; font-size: 16px;'>
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    "It means a ton. I’ve been coming to this stadium for years, and to come and play in front of these fans every weekend is a blessing. All my family was here, so I’m just so proud to put on this jersey. That goal was for my family."
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Eduardo Sosa on the three goal comeback:
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    "No, I’ve never been part of a game like this. It was pretty much a whole lot of offense at the end there and I’ve never been a part of something like that."
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    Michael Bradley had a two minute diatribe about our atmosphere being way behind everyone else last year. Oddly it was after a
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-size: large;">
                   sold out game in Columbus during the playoffs against Toronto.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   Not sure why he felt that was necessary? Or how us being so far behind could be considered true if you look around the rest of MLS?
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    Especially if you checked out a playoff game at Chicago, New York Red Bull, or Houston last year.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    In addition, Revolution, Union, Dynamo, Dallas, Minnesota games couldn't be confused with being at Borussia Dortmund or something? And
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   last time I checked those teams didn't have an owner putting over $2 million dollars into marketing another team that doesn't exist this year.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   So yeah were getting closer to being there this 2018 season but hey thanks Michael Bradley for helping peak the atmosphere so far this year.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-lang="en">
                   <div dir="ltr" lang="en">
                    Karma is a bitch, huh Michael Bradley? Big thumbs up for keeping our undefeated streak going and for helping turn three points into one for your beloved Toronto before seven out of nine games on the road. Real American hero.
                    <a href="https://twitter.com/hashtag/Crew96?src=hash&amp;ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                     #Crew96
                    </a>
                    <a href="https://twitter.com/hashtag/SaveTheCrew?src=hash&amp;ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                     #SaveTheCrew
                    </a>
                    <a href="https://t.co/5YPlek6Zap">
                     pic.twitter.com/5YPlek6Zap
                    </a>
                   </div>
                   — CREWTURE.NET (@crewture)
                   <a href="https://twitter.com/crewture/status/1003096914244579330?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                    June 3, 2018
                   </a>
                  </blockquote>
                  <script async="" charset="utf-8" src="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js">
                  </script>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   Bradley was responsible for all three goals last night.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; color: #343434;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    And the fans were truly right there with the team, willing on the team until the end.
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white;">
                   <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   As even a 60% packed Mapfre can bring it if there in it. No atmosphere? Okay, if you say so. 😏
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   I've seen less passionate crowds at completely sold out MLS games.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   After our first goal, we were dominating so thoroughly that I had oddly little doubt we would come back and get something from this game.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   Sometimes you just know. We have to feel the same way about our eventual success on keeping our team here.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="background-color: white; font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <script type="text/javascript">
                  createSummaryAndThumb("summary1449496620062437541");

           <div class="date-outer">
            <h2 class="date-header">
             <span>
              Friday, June 1, 2018
             </span>
            </h2>
            <div class="date-posts">
             <div class="post-outer">
              <div class="wrapfullpost">
               <div class="post hentry">
                <a name="6420570358733047639">
                </a>
                <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                 <a href="http://www.crewture.net/2018/06/game-preview-despite-very-different.html">
                  GAME PREVIEW: Despite a very different Columbus starting eleven, Toronto's injuries give Columbus chance to keep shutout streak going
                 </a>
                </h3>
                <div class="post-header-line-1">
                </div>
                <div class="postmeta-primary">
                 <span class="meta_date">
                  2:56 AM
                 </span>
                 <span class="meta_categories">
                 </span>

                   <span style="background-color: white;">

                    </span>
                   </span>

                  </span>

                  </span>

                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   So, Ricardo Clark comes in for Wil Trapp and Jon Kempin comes in for Zack Steffen.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Then when someone else in Major League Soccer ref headquarters saw Martinez's clear slap on Sinovic a suspension wasn't far away on the horizon.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   As the refereeing world turns I'm not sure if Federico's red card will get rescinded or should? As should've been a debatable yellow at best but studs up puts yourself in that situation so.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   I guess Columbus could give one of their off-season signings, Eduardo Sosa, who disappeared off the map completely a random first start. But, in a move that makes about zero sense since he usually plays right or left back will likely be Hector Jimenez.

                    <a href="https://twitter.com/hashtag/Crew96?src=hash&amp;ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                     #Crew96
                    </a>
                    <a href="https://t.co/O5G9QbajbJ">
                     https://t.co/O5G9QbajbJ
                    </a>
                    <a href="https://t.co/vioOMTk5jY">
                     pic.twitter.com/vioOMTk5jY
                    </a>
                   </div>
                   — CREWTURE.NET (@crewture)
                   <a href="https://twitter.com/crewture/status/1002175740727758849?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
                    May 31, 2018
                   </a>
                  </blockquote>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <script async="" charset="utf-8" src="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js">
                  </script>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   More of that.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   The Polish Ekstraklasa has a lot of players similar to what Major League Soccer is tapping into in South America currently.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Think a lot of Milton Venezuela's.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   A lot of Polish players could see Major League Soccer as a good next step before making their big move.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Nobody wants to do a Bartosz Kaputska there. The 21 year old went to Leicester City after Euro 2016 at 19 and rarely played, disappeared from the national team as a result.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Major League Soccer could be a good first post-Ekstraklasa move.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                  </span>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   <br/>
                  </span>
                  <b>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    Image of the day:
                   </span>
                  </b>
                  <br/>
                  <b>
                   <span style="font-size: large;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </b>
                  <img src="https://pbs.twimg.com/card_img/1002195013600595975/IBWaZHO7?format=jpg&amp;name=600x314"/>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
                   More like (Shit) Image of the day.
                  </span>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <span style="font-size: large;">
                   Hey make all the renderings your heart desires Anthony Precourt it is not going to happen.
                  </span>
                 </div>

                 </script>
